This may be used to inhibit alerts\n150: // from sending notifications if their meaning is logically a subset of a\n151: // higher-level alert.\n152: type InhibitRule struct {\n153: \t// The set of Filters which define the group of source alerts (which inhibit\n154: \t// the target alerts).\n155: \tSourceMatchers labels.Matchers\n156: \t// The set of Filters which define the group of target alerts (which are\n157: \t// inhibited by the source alerts).\n158: \tTargetMatchers labels.Matchers\n159: \t// A set of label names whose label values need to be identical in source and\n160: \t// target alerts in order for the inhibition to take effect.\n161: \tEqual map[model.LabelName]struct{}\n162: \n163: \t// Cache of alerts matching source labels.\n164: \tscache *store.Alerts\n165: }\n166: \n167: // NewInhibitRule returns a new InhibitRule based on a configuration definition.\n168: func NewInhibitRule(cr config.InhibitRule) *InhibitRule {\n169: \tvar (\n170: \t\tsourcem labels.Matchers\n171: \t\ttargetm labels.Matchers\n172: \t)\n173: \t// cr.SourceMatch will be deprecated. If the snapshot\\n392: // file is set, a snapshot is written to it afterwards.\\n393: // Terminates on receiving from stopc.\\n394: // If not nil, the last argument is an override for what to do as part of the maintenance - for advanced usage.\\n395: func (s *Silences) Maintenance(interval time.Duration, snapf string, stopc <-chan struct{}, override MaintenanceFunc) {\\n396: \\tif interval == 0 || stopc == nil {\\n397: \\t\\ts.logger.Error(\\\"interval or stop signal are missing - not running maintenance\\\")\\n398: \\t\\treturn\\n399: \\t}\\n400: \\tt := s.clock.NewTicker(interval)\\n401: \\tdefer t.Stop()\\n402: \\n403: \\tvar doMaintenance MaintenanceFunc\\n404: \\tdoMaintenance = func() (int64, error) {\\n405: \\t\\tvar size int64\\n406: \\n407: \\t\\tif _, err := s.GC(); This and\\n836: \\t// the use of post-filter functions is the trivial solution for now.\\n837: \\tvar res []*pb.Silence\\n838: \\n839: \\tif q.ids != nil {\\n840: \\t\\tfor _, id := range q.ids {\\n841: \\t\\t\\tif s, ok := s.st[id]; ok {\\n842: \\t\\t\\t\\tres = append(res, s.Silence)\\n843: \\t\\t\\t}\\n844: \\t\\t}\\n845: \\t} else {\\n846: \\t\\tfor _, sil := range s.st {\\n847: \\t\\t\\tres = append(res, sil.Silence)\\n848: \\t\\t}\\n849: \\t}\\n850: \\n851: \\tvar resf []*pb.Silence\\n852: \\tfor _, sil := range res {\\n853: \\t\\tremove := false\\n854: \\t\\tfor _, f := range q.filters {\\n855: \\t\\t\\tok, err := f(sil, s, now)\\n856: \\t\\t\\tif err != nil {\\n857: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn nil, s.version, err\\n858: \\t\\t\\t}\\n859: \\t\\t\\tif !ok {\\n860: \\t\\t\\t\\tremove = true\\n861: \\t\\t\\t\\tbreak\\n862: \\t\\t\\t}\\n863: \\t\\t}\\n864: \\t\\tif !remove {\\n865: \\t\\t\\tresf = append(resf, cloneSilence(sil))\\n866: \\t\\t}\\n867: \\t}\\n868: \\n869: \\treturn resf, s.version, nil\\n870: }\\n871: \\n872: // loadSnapshot loads a snapshot generated by Snapshot() into the state.\\n873: // Any previous state is wiped.\\n874: func (s *Silences) loadSnapshot(r io.Reader) error {\\n875: \\tst, err := decodeState(r)\\n876: \\tif err != nil {\\n877: \\t\\treturn err\\n878: \\t}\\n879: \\tfor _, e := range st {\\n880: \\t\\t// Comments list was moved to a single comment. In other words, the second return is\\n964: // true whenever a silence with a new ID has been added to the state as a result of merge.\\n965: func (s state) merge(e *pb.MeshSilence, now time.Time) (bool, bool) {\\n966: \\tid := e.Silence.Id\\n967: \\tif e.ExpiresAt.Before(now) {\\n968: \\t\\treturn false, false\\n969: \\t}\\n970: \\t// Comments list was moved to a single comment. Muter interface.\n113: func (s *Silencer) Mutes(lset model.LabelSet) bool {\n114: \tfp := lset.Fingerprint()\n115: \tactiveIDs, pendingIDs, markerVersion, _ := s.marker.Silenced(fp)\n116: \n117: \tvar (\n118: \t\terr        error\n119: \t\tallSils    []*pb.Silence\n120: \t\tnewVersion = markerVersion\n121: \t)\n122: \tif markerVersion == s.silences.Version() {\n123: \t\ttotalSilences := len(activeIDs) + len(pendingIDs)\n124: \t\t// No new silences added, just need to check which of the old\n125: \t\t// silences are still relevant and which of the pending ones\n126: \t\t// have become active.\n127: \t\tif totalSilences == 0 {\n128: \t\t\t// Super fast path: No silences ever applied to this\n129: \t\t\t// alert, none have been added. We are done.\n130: \t\t\treturn false\n131: \t\t}\n132: \t\t// This is still a quite fast path: No silences have been added,\n133: \t\t// we only need to check which of the applicable silences are\n134: \t\t// currently active. So let's do it in any case. Note that we cannot reuse the\n161: \t// current ID slices for concurrency reasons.\n162: \tactiveIDs, pendingIDs = nil, nil\n163: \tnow := s.silences.nowUTC()\n164: \tfor _, sil := range allSils \tsort.Strings(pendingIDs)\n183: \n184: \ts.marker.SetActiveOrSilenced(fp, newVersion, activeIDs, pendingIDs)\n185: \n186: \treturn len(activeIDs) > 0\n187: }\n188: \n189: // Silences holds a silence \t\t)\n317: \t}\n318: \treturn m\n319: }\n320: \n321: // Options exposes configuration options for creating a new Silences object.\n322: // Its zero value is a safe default.\n323: type Options struct {\n324: \t// A snapshot file or reader from which the initial state is loaded.\n325: \t// None or only one of them must be set.\n326: \tSnapshotFile   string\n327: \tSnapshotReader io.Reader\n328: \n329: \t// Retention time for newly created Silences. Silences may be\n330: \t// garbage collected after the given duration after they ended.\n331: \tRetention time.Duration\n332: \tLimits    Limits\n333: \n334: \t// A logger used by background processing.\n335: \tLogger  *slog.Logger\n336: \tMetrics prometheus.Registerer\n337: }\n338: \n339: func (o *Options) validate() error {\n340: \tif o.SnapshotFile != \"\" && o.SnapshotReader != nil {\n341: \t\treturn errors.New(\"only one of SnapshotFile and SnapshotReader must be set\")\n342: \t}\n343: \treturn nil\n344: }\n345: \n346: // New returns a new Silences object with the given configuration.\n347: func New(o Options) (*Silences, error) {\n348: \tif err := o.validate(); err != nil {\n349: \t\treturn nil, err\n350: \t}\n351: \n352: \ts := &Silences{\n353: \t\tclock:     quartz.NewReal(),\n354: \t\tmc:        matcherCache{},\n355: \t\tlogger:    promslog.NewNopLogger(),\n356: \t\tretention: o.Retention,\n357: \t\tlimits:    o.Limits,\n358: \t\tbroadcast: func([]byte) {},\n359: \t\tst:        state{},\n360: \t}\n361: \ts.metrics = newMetrics(o.Metrics, s)\n362: \n363: \tif o.Logger != nil {\n364: \t\ts.logger = o.Logger\n365: \t}\n366: \n367: \tif o.SnapshotFile != \"\" {\n368: \t\tif r, err := os.Open(o.SnapshotFile); err != nil {\n369: \t\t\tif !os.IsNotExist(err) {\n370: \t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n371: \t\t\t}\n372: \t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"silences snapshot file doesn't exist\", \"err\", err)\n373: \t\t} else {\n374: \t\t\to.SnapshotReader = r\n375: \t\t\tdefer r.Close()\n376: \t\t}\n377: \t}\n378: \n379: \tif o.SnapshotReader != nil {\n380: \t\tif err := s.loadSnapshot(o.SnapshotReader); err != nil {\n381: \t\t\treturn s, err\n382: \t\t}\n383: \t}\n384: \treturn s, nil\n385: }\n386: \n387: func (s *Silences) nowUTC() time.Time {\n388: \treturn s.clock.Now().UTC()\n389: }\n390: \n391: // Maintenance garbage collects the silence state at the given interval. If the snapshot\n392: // file is set, a snapshot is written to it afterwards.\n393: // Terminates on receiving from stopc.\n394: // If not nil, the last argument is an override for what to do as part of the maintenance - for advanced usage.\n395: func (s *Silences) Maintenance(interval time.Duration, snapf string, stopc <-chan struct{}, override MaintenanceFunc) {\n396: \tif interval == 0 || stopc == nil {\n397: \t\ts.logger.Error(\"interval or stop signal are missing - not running maintenance\")\n398: \t\treturn\n399: \t}\n400: \tt := s.clock.NewTicker(interval)\n401: \tdefer t.Stop()\n402: \n403: \tvar doMaintenance MaintenanceFunc\n404: \tdoMaintenance = func() (int64, error) {\n405: \t\tvar size int64\n406: \n407: \t\tif _, err := s.GC(); err != nil {\n408: \t\t\treturn size, err\n409: \t\t}\n410: \t\tif snapf == \"\" {\n411: \t\t\treturn size, nil\n412: \t\t}\n413: \t\tf, err := openReplace(snapf)\n414: \t\tif err != nil {\n415: \t\t\treturn size, err\n416: \t\t}\n417: \t\tif size, err = s.Snapshot(f); err != nil {\n418: \t\t\tf.Close()\n419: \t\t\treturn size, err\n420: \t\t}\n421: \t\treturn size, f.Close()\n422: \t}\n423: \n424: \tif override != nil {\n425: \t\tdoMaintenance = override\n426: \t}\n427: \n428: \trunMaintenance := func(do MaintenanceFunc) error {\n429: \t\ts.metrics.maintenanceTotal.Inc()\n430: \t\ts.logger.Debug(\"Running maintenance\")\n431: \t\tstart := s.nowUTC()\n432: \t\tsize, err := do()\n433: \t\ts.metrics.snapshotSize.Set(float64(size))\n434: \t\tif err != nil {\n435: \t\t\ts.metrics.maintenanceErrorsTotal.Inc()\n436: \t\t\treturn err\n437: \t\t}\n438: \t\ts.logger.Debug(\"Maintenance done\", \"duration\", s.clock.Since(start), \"size\", size)\n439: \t\treturn nil\n440: \t}\n441: \n442: Loop:\n443: \tfor {\n444: \t\tselect {\n445: \t\tcase <-stopc:\n446: \t\t\tbreak Loop\n447: \t\tcase <-t.C:\n448: \t\t\tif err := runMaintenance(doMaintenance); err != nil {\n449: \t\t\t\t// @tjhop: this should probably log at error level\n450: \t\t\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Running maintenance failed\", \"err\", err)\n451: \t\t\t}\n452: \t\t}\n453: \t}\n454: \n455: \t// No need for final maintenance if we don't want to snapshot.\n456: \tif snapf == \"\" {\n457: \t\treturn\n458: \t}\n459: \tif err := runMaintenance(doMaintenance); err != nil {\n460: \t\t// @tjhop: this should probably log at error level\n461: \t\ts.logger.Info(\"Creating shutdown snapshot failed\", \"err\", err)\n462: \t}\n463: }\n464: \n465: // GC runs a garbage collection that removes silences that have ended longer\n466: // than the configured retention time ago.\n467: func (s *Silences) GC() (int, error) {\n468: \tstart := time.Now()\n469: \tdefer func() { s.metrics.gcDuration.Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds()) }()\n470: \n471: \tnow := s.nowUTC()\n472: \tvar n int\n473: \n474: \ts.mtx.Lock()\n475: \tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\n476: \n477: \tfor id, sil := range s.st {\n478: \t\tif sil.ExpiresAt.IsZero() {\n479: \t\t\treturn n, errors.New(\"unexpected zero expiration timestamp\")\n480: \t\t}\n481: \t\tif !sil.ExpiresAt.After(now) {\n482: \t\t\tdelete(s.st, id)\n483: \t\t\tdelete(s.mc, sil.Silence.Id)\n484: \t\t\tn++\n485: \t\t}\n486: \t}\n487: \n488: \treturn n, nil\n489: }\n490: \n491: func validateMatcher(m *pb.Matcher) error {\n492: \tif !compat.IsValidLabelName(model.LabelName(m.Name)) {\n493: \t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label name %q\", m.Name)\n494: \t}\n495: \tswitch m.Type {\n496: \tcase pb.Matcher_EQUAL, pb.Matcher_NOT_EQUAL:\n497: \t\tif !model.LabelValue(m.Pattern).IsValid() {\n498: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label value %q\", m.Pattern)\n499: \t\t}\n500: \tcase pb.Matcher_REGEXP, pb.Matcher_NOT_REGEXP:\n501: \t\tif _, err := regexp.Compile(m.Pattern); If a silence with the ID already exists and the modification\n594: // modifies history, the old silence gets expired and a new one is created.\n595: func (s *Silences) Set(sil *pb.Silence) error {\n596: \ts.mtx.Lock()\n597: \tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\n598: \n599: \tnow := s.nowUTC()\n600: \tif sil.StartsAt.IsZero() {\n601: \t\tsil.StartsAt = now\n602: \t}\n603: \n604: \tif err := \t\treturn ErrNotFound\n611: \t}\n612: \n613: \tif ok && canUpdate(prev, sil, now) {\n614: \t\tsil.UpdatedAt = now\n615: \t\tmsil := s.toMeshSilence(sil)\n616: \t\tif err := s.checkSizeLimits(msil); err != nil {\n617: \t\t\treturn err\n618: \t\t}\n619: \t\treturn s.setSilence(msil, now)\n620: \t}\n621: \n622: \t// If we got here it's either a new silence or a replacing one (which would\n623: \t// also create a new silence) so we need to make sure we have capacity for\n624: \t// the new silence.\n625: \tif s.limits.MaxSilences != nil {\n626: \t\tif m := s.limits.MaxSilences(); m > 0 && len(s.st)+1 > m {\n627: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"exceeded maximum number of silences: %d (limit: %d)\", len(s.st), m)\n628: \t\t}\n629: \t}\n630: \n631: \tuid, err := uuid.NewV4()\n632: \tif err != nil {\n633: \t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"generate uuid: %w\", err)\n634: \t}\n635: \tsil.Id = uid.String()\n636: \n637: \tif sil.StartsAt.Before(now) {\n638: \t\tsil.StartsAt = now\n639: \t}\n640: \tsil.UpdatedAt = now\n641: \n642: \tmsil := s.toMeshSilence(sil)\n643: \tif err := s.checkSizeLimits(msil); err != nil {\n644: \t\treturn err\n645: \t}\n646: \n647: \tif ok && getState(prev, s.nowUTC()) != types.SilenceStateExpired {\n648: \t\t// We cannot update the silence, expire the old one to leave a history of\n649: \t\t// the silence before modification.\n650: \t\tif err := s.expire(prev.Id); err != nil {\n651: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expire previous silence: %w\", err)\n652: \t\t}\n653: \t}\n654: \n655: \treturn s.setSilence(msil, now)\n656: }\n657: \n658: // canUpdate returns true if silence a can be updated to b without\n659: // affecting the historic view of silencing.\n660: func canUpdate(a, b *pb.Silence, now time.Time) bool {\n661: \tif !reflect.DeepEqual(a.Matchers, b.Matchers) {\n662: \t\treturn false\n663: \t}\n664: \t// Allowed timestamp modifications depend on the current time.\n665: \tswitch st := getState(a, now); st {\n666: \tdefault:\n680: \t\tpanic(\"unknown silence state\")\n681: \t}\n682: \treturn true\n683: }\n684: \n685: // Expire the silence with the given ID immediately.\n686: func (s *Silences) Expire(id string) returned if the silence already expired before it is GC'd.\n694: // If the silence is not found an error is returned.\n695: func (s *Silences) expire(id string) error {\n696: \tsil, ok := s.getSilence(id)\n697: \tif !ok {\n698: \t\treturn ErrNotFound\n699: \t}\n700: \tsil = cloneSilence(sil)\n701: \tnow := s.nowUTC()\n702: \n703: \tswitch getState(sil, now) {\n704: \tcase This and\n836: \t// the use of post-filter functions is the trivial solution for now.\n837: \tvar res []*pb.Silence\n838: \n839: \tif q.ids != nil {\n840: \t\tfor _, id := range q.ids {\n841: \t\t\tif s, ok := s.st[id]; ok {\n842: \t\t\t\tres = append(res, s.Silence)\n843: \t\t\t}\n844: \t\t}\n845: \t} else {\n846: \t\tfor _, sil := range s.st {\n847: \t\t\tres = append(res, sil.Silence)\n848: \t\t}\n849: \t}\n850: \n851: \tvar resf []*pb.Silence\n852: \tfor _, sil := range res {\n853: \t\tremove := false\n854: \t\tfor _, f := range q.filters {\n855: \t\t\tok, err := f(sil, s, now)\n856: \t\t\tif err != nil {\n857: \t\t\t\treturn nil, s.version, err\n858: \t\t\t}\n859: \t\t\tif !ok {\n860: \t\t\t\tremove = true\n861: \t\t\t\tbreak\n862: \t\t\t}\n863: \t\t}\n864: \t\tif !remove {\n865: \t\t\tresf = append(resf, cloneSilence(sil))\n866: \t\t}\n867: \t}\n868: \n869: \treturn resf, s.version, nil\n870: }\n871: \n872: // loadSnapshot loads a snapshot generated by Snapshot() into the state.\n873: // Any previous state is wiped.\n874: func (s *Silences) loadSnapshot(r io.Reader) error {\n875: \tst, err := decodeState(r)\n876: \tif err != nil {\n877: \t\treturn err\n878: \t}\n879: \tfor _, e := range st {\n880: \t\t// Comments list was moved to a single comment. We don't\n941: \t\t\t\t// propagate oversized messages because they're sent to\n942: \t\t\t\t// all nodes already.\n943: \t\t\t\ts.broadcast(b)\n944: \t\t\t\ts.metrics.propagatedMessagesTotal.Inc()\n945: \t\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"Gossiping new silence\", \"silence\", e)\n946: \t\t\t}\n947: \t\t}\n948: \t}\n949: \treturn nil\n950: }\n951: \n952: // SetBroadcast sets the provided function as the one creating data to be\n953: // broadcast.\n954: func (s *Silences) SetBroadcast(f func([]byte)) {\n955: \ts.mtx.Lock()\n956: \ts.broadcast = f\n957: \ts.mtx.Unlock()\n958: }\n959: \n960: type state map[string]*pb.MeshSilence\n961: \n962: // merge returns two bools: the first is true when merge caused a state change. The second\n963: // is true if that state change added a new silence. In other words, the second return is\n964: // true whenever a silence with a new ID has been added to the state as a result of merge.\n965: func (s state) merge(e *pb.MeshSilence, now time.Time) (bool, bool) {\n966: \tid := e.Silence.Id\n967: \tif e.ExpiresAt.Before(now) {\n968: \t\treturn false, false\n969: \t}\n970: \t// Comments list was moved to a single comment. It implements a subscription pattern by calling alerts.Subscribe() to receive incoming alerts. In the run() method (line 148), it iterates through each alert and uses d.route.Match(alert.Labels) to find all matching routes in the routing tree. The routing tree is defined in dispatch/route.go as a Route structure with hierarchical matching rules. Each matched route is passed to processAlert(), which determines the aggregation group for the alert and schedules notifications.\\n\\n## Inhibition Check\\nThe inhibit/inhibit.go Inhibitor component evaluates inhibition rules to suppress notifications for target alerts when source alerts are firing. The Inhibitor.Mutes() method (line 127) checks if an alert's label set matches any inhibition rule's target side, and if the source alerts of that rule are currently active. Inhibition rules are defined with source and target matchers, and require matching label values specified in the Equal field. The inhibitor runs in the background to maintain a cache of active source alerts.\\n\\n## Silence Check  \\nThe silence/silence.go Silencer component checks if alerts are silenced. TimeActiveStage - checks active time intervals  \\n4. TimeMuteStage - checks mute time intervals\\n5. MuteStage with Silencer (line 411) - filters silenced alerts\\n6. Per-receiver stages created by createReceiverStage() (lines 424-447) for actual notification delivery\\n\\nEach Stage implements the Stage interface (line 243) with an Exec method that transforms the alert list and context as it passes through the pipeline.\\n\\n## Final Notifier Dispatch\\nAfter passing through all stages, alerts reach the per-receiver integration stages.
